   <!--Cookie Consent Bar by iSenseLabs GDPR Extension-->
   <script>
    var analytics_cookies_disable = '_ga,_gid,_gat,__atuvc,__atuvs,__utma,__cfduid';
 		var marketing_cookies_disable = '_gads,IDE,test_cookie,fr,tr,collect,GPS,PREF,BizoID';
 		var disabled_cookie_sets = '';
 		var url_variations = JSON.parse('[".www.da-teatro.com","www.da-teatro.com",".da-teatro.com","da-teatro.com"]');
 		var disable_marketing = false;
 		var disable_analytics = false;
 		
 		var set_gdpr_handlers = function(){
 			 
 			$('body').delegate('a.cc-btn.cc-allow', 'click', function(e) {
 				$.get('https://www.da-teatro.com/index.php?route=extension/module/isenselabs_gdpr/accept_pp_from_ccb');
 			});
 						$('body').delegate('a.cc-btn.cc-dismiss', 'click', function(e) {
 				 
 					// return false;
 				 
 			});
 			
 			$('body').delegate('a.cc-btn-close-settings', 'click', function(e) {
 				$('.cc-settings-view').fadeOut(100);
 			});
 			$('body').delegate('a.cc-btn-save-settings', 'click', function(e) {
 				var cookie_text = '';
 				if ($('input[name="cookie_isl_analytics"]:checked').length == 0) {
 					cookie_text += 'analytics,';
 				}
 				if ($('input[name="cookie_isl_marketing"]:checked').length == 0) {
 					cookie_text += 'marketing,';
 				}
 				Cookies.set('cookieconsent_preferences_disabled', cookie_text, { expires: 365 });
 				$('.cc-settings-view').fadeToggle(100);
 			});
 		};
 		
 		function maintainCookies() {
 			if (disabled_cookie_sets.indexOf('marketing') >= 0) disable_marketing = true;
 			if (disabled_cookie_sets.indexOf('analytics') >= 0) disable_analytics = true;
 			$.each(Cookies.get(), function(i, item) {
 				if (disable_analytics && (analytics_cookies_disable.indexOf(i) >= 0)) {
 					$.each(url_variations, function(ai, asite) {
 						clearCookie(i,asite,'/');
 					});
 				}
 				if (disable_marketing && (marketing_cookies_disable.indexOf(i) >= 0)) {
 					$.each(url_variations, function(mi, msite) {
 						clearCookie(i,msite,'/');
 					});
 				}
 			});
 			return true;
 		}
 		
 		var cc_popup;
 		window.addEventListener("load", function(){
 			cookieconsent.initialise({
 			   
 			   
 			  "palette": {
 				"popup": {
 				  "background": "#000000",
 				  "text": "#ffffff"
 				},
 				"button": {
 				  "background": "#800000",
 				  "text": "#ffffff"
 				}
 			  },
 			  "type": "opt-in",
 			   
 			  "alwaysShow": false,  
 			   
 			   
 			  "content": {
 				"message": "DaTeatro usa i Cookies per fornirti la migliore esperienza possibile. Proseguendo la navigazione o cliccando su accetta acconsenti all'utilizzo dei Cookies.",
 				"allow": "Accetta",
 				"dismiss": "Chiudi",
 				"settings": "Modifica Preferenze",
 				 
 				"link": "Leggi l'Informativa Privacy e Cookies",
 				"href": "https://www.da-teatro.com/privacy-e-cookies"
 				 
 			  }
 			}, function (popup) {
 				cc_popup = popup;
 			}, function (err) {
 				console.log(err);
 			});
 			
 			var html_cookie_settings = '<div id="cookieconsent:settings" class="cc-settings-view"><div class="cc-settings-dialog"><span class="cookie_settings_header">Seleziona il tipo di cookies che accetti</span><br /><br /><label><input type="checkbox" checked="checked" disabled="disabled" value="functional" /> Cookies strettamente necessari</label><br />Cookies indispensabili al funzionamento del sito. Tali cookies vengono impostati solo in risposta alle azioni eseguite come lingua, valuta, sessione di accesso, preferenze. Puoi impostare il tuo browser per bloccare questi cookies ma il nostro sito potrebbe non funzionare.<br /><br /><label><input type="checkbox"  name="cookie_isl_analytics" value="analytics" /> Analitici e statistici</label><br />Questi cookies ci permettono di misurare il traffico dei visitatori e vedere le sorgenti di traffico raccogliendo informazioni in insiemi di dati. Inoltre ci aiutano a capire quali prodotti e azioni sono pi&ugrave; popolari di altri.<br /><br /><label><input type="checkbox"  name="cookie_isl_marketing" value="marketing" /> Marketing e retargeting (profilazione)</label><br />Questi cookies sono solitamente impostati da partner di marketing e pubblicitari per creare un profilo di tuo interesse per mostrare annunci pertinenti. Disabilitando questi cookies non si verificheranno annunci mirati per i propri interessi.<br /><br /><div class="cc-compliance cc-highlight"><a class="cc-btn cc-btn-close-settings">X chiudi</a>&nbsp;&nbsp;<a class="cc-btn cc-btn-save-settings">Salva</a></div></div></div>';
 			$('body').append(html_cookie_settings);
 			set_gdpr_handlers();
 			maintainCookies();
 		});
   </script>

   <div class="hide hidden-data">
    <input name="model" value="1"/>
    <input name="image" value="1"/>
    <input name="price" value="0"/>
    <input name="addtocart" value="0"/>
    <input name="view_all_results" value="Guarda tutti i risultati"/>
    <input name="no_results_found" value="Nessun risultato"/>
    <input name="button_cart" value="Acquista"/>

   <script type="text/javascript">
    $(document).ready(function() {
 	$('#search').find('input[name=\'search\']').wautocomplete({
 		source: function(request, response) {
 			$.ajax({
 				url: 'index.php?route=extension/wsearch/autocomplete&filter_name='+encodeURIComponent(request),
 				dataType: 'json',
 				success: function(json) {
 					response($.map(json, function(item) {
 						return {
 							price:   item.price,
 							special: item.special,
 							model: item.model,
 							label:   item.name,
 							image:   item.image,
 							link:    item.link,
 							minimum:    item.minimum,
 							value:   item.product_id,
 						}
 					}));
 				}
 			});
 		},
 
 	});
 });
 
 // Autocomplete */
 (function($) {
 	$.fn.wautocomplete = function(option) {
 		return this.each(function() {
 			var $this = $(this);
 			var $dropdown = $('<ul class="dropdown-menu" />');
 
 			this.timer = null;
 			this.items = [];
 
 			$.extend(this, option);
 
 			$this.attr('autocomplete', 'off');
 
 			// Focus
 			/* $this.on('focus', function() {
 				this.request();
 			}); */
 
 			// Blur
 			$this.on('blur', function() {
 				setTimeout(function(object) {
 					object.hide();
 				}, 200, this);
 			});
 
 			// Keydown
 			$this.on('keydown', function(event) {
 				switch(event.keyCode) {
 					case 27: // escape
 						this.hide();
 						break;
 					default:
 						this.request();
 						break;
 				}
 			});
 
 			// Click
 			this.click = function(event) {
 				event.preventDefault();
 
 				var value = $(event.target).parent().attr('data-value');
 
 				if (value && this.items[value]) {
 					this.select(this.items[value]);
 				}
 			}
 
 			// Show
 			this.show = function() {
 				var pos = $this.position();
 
 				$dropdown.css({
 					top: pos.top + $this.outerHeight(),
 					left: pos.left
 				});
 
 				$dropdown.show();
 			}
 
 			// Hide
 			this.hide = function() {
 				$dropdown.hide();
 			}
 
 			// Request
 			this.request = function() {
 				clearTimeout(this.timer);
 
 				this.timer = setTimeout(function(object) {
 					object.source($(object).val(), $.proxy(object.response, object));
 				}, 200, this);
 			}
 
 			// Response
 			this.response = function(json) {
 				var html = '';
 				var show_model = $('.hidden-data input[name="model"]').val();
 				var show_price = $('.hidden-data input[name="price"]').val();
 				var show_image = $('.hidden-data input[name="image"]').val();
 				var show_addtocart = $('.hidden-data input[name="addtocart"]').val();
 				var view_all_results = $('.hidden-data input[name="view_all_results"]').val();
 				var no_results_found = $('.hidden-data input[name="no_results_found"]').val();
 				var button_cart = $('.hidden-data input[name="button_cart"]').val();
 
 				if (json.length) {
 					for (i = 0; i < json.length; i++) {
 						// update element items
 						this.items[json[i]['value']] = json[i];
 					}
 					
 					for (j = 0; j < json.length; j++) {
 						html += '<li class="media searchproducts" data-value="' + json[j]['value'] + '">';
 							if(json[j]['image'] && show_image == '1') {
 								html += '	<a class="media-left pull-left" href="' + json[j]['link'] + '"><img class="pull-left" src="' + json[j]['image'] + '"></a>';	
 							}
 							html += '<div class="media-body">';	
 							html += '<div class="pull-left">';	
 							html += '<a href="' + json[j]['link'] + '" class="product_name"><strong>' + json[j]['label'] + '</strong></a><br>';
 							if(show_model == '1') {
 								html += '<span class="product_model">Model: ' + json[j]['model'] + '</span>';
 							}
 							html += '</div>';
 							html += '<div class="pull-right">';	
 							if(json[j]['price'] && show_price == '1'){
 								html += '	<div class="price">';
 							if (!json[j]['special']) {
 								html += '<span class="price">'+json[j]['price']+'</span>';
 							} else {
 								html += '<span class="price-new">' + json[j]['special'] + '</span>';
 							}
 								html += '	</div>';
 							}
 							if(show_addtocart == '1'){
 								html += '<a type="button" class="btn btn-primary pull-right btn-addcart" onclick="cart.add(' + json[j]['value'] + ',' + json[j]['minimum'] + ');"><span>'+ button_cart +'</span> </a>';
 							}
 							html += '</div>';
 							html += '</div>';
 							html += '</li>';
 							html += '<li class="clearfix"></li>';
 					}
 					html += '<li class="allresults"><a>'+ view_all_results +'</a></li>';
 				}else{
 					html += '<li class="media searchproducts">';
 					html += '<div class="media-body">';	
 					html += '<p class="text-center noresults">'+ no_results_found +'</p>';
 					html += '</div>';
 					html += '</li>';
 				}
 
 				if (html) {
 					this.show();
 				} else {
 					this.hide();
 				}
 
 				$dropdown.html(html);
 				$('.allresults a').on('click', function() {
 					$('#search span button').trigger('click');
 				});
 			}
 
 			$dropdown.on('click', '> li > a', $.proxy(this.click, this));
 			$this.after($dropdown);
 			
 		});
 	}
 })(window.jQuery);
   </script>
